### [1] [Effective rates for continuous-time quasi-Fejér monotone dynamical systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23708)
*Anton Freund,Nicholas Pischke*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 论文为满足拟Fejér单调性连续时间版本的度量空间动力系统提供了定量收敛结果，包括紧度量空间的收敛速率构造和非紧空间的推广，并展示了该理论在多种动力系统中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究满足连续时间拟Fejér单调性的动力系统的定量收敛理论，为这类系统建立统一的收敛分析框架，克服传统定性分析的局限性，提供可计算的收敛速率。

Method: 采用定量分析方法，为紧度量空间中的连续时间拟Fejér单调系统构造显式的连续时间元稳定性速率；通过正则性假设将结果推广到非紧空间；通过模数表示系统关键属性的定量见证和空间的紧致性度量。

Result: 获得了紧度量空间中动力系统的强收敛结果，构造了显式且有效的连续时间元稳定性速率；在正则性条件下将收敛结果扩展到非紧空间，并能构造类似的均匀收敛速率；证明了该理论在希尔伯特空间中的经典一阶和二阶动力系统、非线性Hadamard空间中的（广义）梯度流及相关半群等案例中的适用性。

Conclusion: 连续时间拟Fejér单调性为多种动力系统和微分方程提供了统一的收敛分析框架，所建立的定量理论不仅具有理论新颖性，而且在实际应用中能够提供可计算的收敛速率，为动力系统的定量分析提供了系统的方法论。

Abstract: We provide quantitative convergence results for continuous-time dynamical systems in metric spaces that satisfy a continuous-time analog of quasi-Fejér monotonicity. More precisely, we provide a (strong) convergence result for such dynamical systems over compact metric spaces which is quantitatively outfitted with a continuous-time rate of metastability, which moreover can be explicitly and effectively constructed in a very uniform way, only depending on a few moduli representing quantitative witnesses to key properties of the dynamical system and a measure for the compactness of the space. We further show how this convergence result can be extended to non-compact spaces under a regularity assumption of the associated problem, where moreover rates of convergence can then be explicitly constructed which are similarly uniform. In both cases, already the associated ``infinitary'' convergence result is qualitatively novel in its present generality. Beyond this abstract quantitative theory for such dynamical systems, we motivate how the presently studied continuous-time variant of quasi-Fejér monotonicity naturally occurs as a unifying property of many dynamical systems and differential equations and inclusions, and in that way can be used to provide a comprehensive quantitative theory for many such dynamical systems. We illustrate this with three case studies for both classical first- and second-order dynamical systems in Hilbert spaces as well as (generalized) gradient flows and associated semigroups in nonlinear Hadamard spaces.

</details>


### [2] [Risk-Aware Linear-Quadratic Regulation with Temporally Coupled States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23737)
*Chuanning Wei,Kin Fung Li,Dionysis Kalogerias,Margaret P. Chapman*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种在有限时域内考虑时间变异性和随机变异性的离散时间LQR问题，通过扩展预测方差风险度量来处理时间耦合状态，实现了状态调节与时间变异性之间的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统LQR控制主要关注状态调节，但实际应用中还需要考虑状态轨迹的时间变异性和随机变异性。现有方法缺乏对时间耦合状态下风险敏感性的明确处理，需要开发能够平衡状态调节与时间变异性、同时考虑风险敏感性的控制框架。

Method: 扩展预测方差风险度量到时间耦合状态设置，构建有限时域离散时间LQR问题，同时惩罚状态的时间变异性和随机变异性。通过数学公式化处理时间耦合效应，实现风险敏感控制。

Result: 数值实验展示了时间耦合在风险感知和风险中性控制设置中的影响。特别发现，仅显式惩罚时间变异性也能减少随机变异性，表明时间变异性惩罚具有双重效益。

Conclusion: 提出的框架成功实现了状态调节与时间变异性之间的平衡，并提供了明确的风险敏感性。扩展的预测方差风险度量有效处理了时间耦合状态，为风险感知控制提供了新工具。

Abstract: We formulate and solve a discrete-time linear-quadratic regulation (LQR) problem in a finite horizon that penalizes temporal variability and stochastic variability of the state trajectory. Our approach enables the user to strike a balance between regulating the state and reducing temporal variability, with explicit sensitivity to risk. We achieve this by extending a risk measure called predictive variance to a setting with temporally coupled states. Numerical examples demonstrate the effect of temporal coupling in both risk-aware and risk-neutral control settings. Particularly, we observe that explicitly penalizing temporal variability alone can also reduce stochastic variability.

</details>


### [3] [Accelerating Low-Frequency Convergence for Limited-Angle DBT via Two-Channel Fidelity in PDHG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23955)
*Taro Iyadomi,Ricardo Parada,Anna Kim,Lily Jiang,Emil Sidky,William Chang*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出一种用于有限角度数字乳腺断层合成重建的双通道保真度策略，通过将正弦图残差分解为互补的低通和高通频带，使用独立约束和双变量更新来加速低频分量的收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有限角度数字乳腺断层合成重建中，使用加权数据保真度项时，低空间频率分量的收敛速度较慢，这影响了重建质量和效率。

Method: 采用双通道保真度策略，使用平方根汉宁滤波器族将正弦图残差分解为互补的低通和高通频带。每个频带使用独立的ℓ_2球约束，在带有He-Yuan预测器-校正器松弛的PDHG算法中进行独立的双变量更新。为低频通道分配更大的双步长和稍宽松的容差。

Result: 在2D数字乳腺体模上的多分辨率实验表明，双通道方法相比单通道基线实现了19%--61%的RMSE改进。在更粗糙的离散化条件下（问题条件更有利时）获得更大的增益。

Conclusion: 双通道保真度策略能够在临床现实的有限角度条件下实现更平衡的频谱收敛，通过更强的每迭代校正来加速低频分量的收敛，同时不违反全局PDHG稳定性。

Abstract: Reconstruction in limited-angle digital breast tomosynthesis (DBT) suffers from slow convergence of low spatial-frequency components when using weighted data-fidelity terms within primal-dual optimization. We introduce a two-channel fidelity strategy that decomposes the sinogram residual into complementary low-pass and high-pass bands using square-root Hanning (Hann^{1/2}) filter families, each driven by an independent \ell_2-ball constraint and dual update in the PDHG (Chambolle-Pock) algorithm with He-Yuan predictor-corrector relaxation. By assigning a larger dual step size and slightly looser tolerance to the low-frequency channel, the method delivers stronger per-iteration correction to the near-DC band without violating global PDHG stability. Experiments on a 2D digital breast phantom across multiple resolutions demonstrate that the two-channel approach yields 19%--61% RMSE improvement over the single-channel baseline, with larger gains at coarser discretizations where problem conditioning is more favorable, supporting more balanced spectral convergence in clinically realistic limited-angle regimes.

</details>


### [4] [Utility-Invariant Support Selection and Eventwise Decoupling for Simultaneous Independent Multi-Outcome Bets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24064)
*Christopher D. Long*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 论文证明了在有限结果的同时独立事件中，对于非负赌注和内生现金头寸的期望效用问题，存在一个短支撑定理：最优投资组合的活跃支撑是各事件单事件支撑的并集，且该支撑与效用函数无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究同时独立事件下的期望效用最大化问题，其中赌注非负且现金头寸内生。目标是理解最优投资组合的支撑结构特性，特别是支撑如何与效用函数无关。

Method: 通过分析一阶条件，推导出关键恒等式 λ/K_ℓ^(U) = (1-P_ℓ,A)/(1-Q_ℓ,A)，其中P_ℓ,A和Q_ℓ,A分别是事件ℓ的活跃概率质量和价格质量，λ是预算乘子，K_ℓ^(U)是延续因子。通过按边缘比p_ℓi/π_ℓi排序每个事件，证明活跃支撑是各事件单事件支撑的并集。

Result: 证明了短支撑定理：对于一大类严格递增严格凹的效用函数，最优投资组合的活跃支撑是各事件单事件支撑的并集，且该支撑独立于具体的效用函数。这扩展了Smoczynski和Miles在自由暴露同注分彩设定中的结果。

Conclusion: 在同时独立事件框架下，一旦识别出正确的延续因子，最优投资组合的支撑结构具有与单事件情况相同的状态价格几何性质，支撑是效用不变的且由各事件的单事件支撑并集构成。

Abstract: For simultaneous independent events with finitely many outcomes, consider the expected-utility problem with nonnegative wagers and an endogenous cash position. We prove a short support theorem for a broad class of strictly increasing strictly concave utilities. On any fixed support family and at any optimal portfolio with positive cash, summing the active first-order conditions and comparing that sum with cash stationarity yields the exact identity \[ \fracλ{K_{\ell}^{(U)}}=\frac{1-P_{\ell,A}}{1-Q_{\ell,A}}, \] where $P_{\ell,A}$ and $Q_{\ell,A}$ are the active probability and price masses of event $\ell$, $λ$ is the budget multiplier, and $K_{\ell}^{(U)}$ is the continuation factor seen by inactive outcomes of that event. Consequently, after sorting each event by the edge ratio $p_{\ell i}/π_{\ell i}$, the exact active support is the eventwise union of the single-event supports, and this support is independent of the utility function. The single-event utility-invariant support theorem is already explicit in the free-exposure pari-mutuel setting in Smoczynski and Miles; the point of the present note is that the simultaneous independent-events analogue follows from the same state-price geometry once the right continuation factor is identified.

</details>


### [5] [Theoretical properties of the eigenvector method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24274)
*Sándor Bozóki,László Csató*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文讨论了右特征向量作为成对比较矩阵权重推导方法的五个潜在缺陷：左右不对称性、群体选择不一致性、偏好强度依赖性、权重反直觉变化以及帕累托非效率性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管右特征向量是成对比较矩阵权重推导的经典方法，但文献已识别出其多个理论缺陷。本文旨在系统分析这些潜在弱点，为决策分析领域提供更全面的方法评估。

Method: 通过理论分析和反例说明的方法，系统探讨右特征向量方法的五个具体问题：1) 左右特征向量不对称性；2) 群体决策中的选择不一致性；3) 偏好强度对排序的影响；4) 权重反直觉变化；5) 帕累托效率缺失。

Result: 右特征向量方法存在五个明确的缺陷：1) 左右特征向量不一致导致不对称性；2) 个体权重聚合与矩阵聚合的排序可能不同；3) 偏好强度变化会影响排序结果；4) 特定比较的修改可能导致权重反直觉变化；5) 可能存在帕累托更优的权重向量。

Conclusion: 右特征向量作为成对比较矩阵权重推导方法存在多个理论缺陷，需要通过反例和理论分析加以认识。本文提出了未来研究的开放性问题，为改进决策分析方法提供了方向。

Abstract: A classical proposal to derive weights from a pairwise comparison matrix is the right eigenvector. The literature has identified some potential weaknesses of this method in previous decades. This chapter discusses five of these issues. First, right-left asymmetry emerges because of the difference between the right and inverse left eigenvectors. Second, group incoherence for choice means that, in group decision-making problems, the ranking given by the aggregated individual weight vectors is not guaranteed to coincide with the ranking derived from the aggregated pairwise comparison matrix. Third, the ranking based on the right eigenvector may depend on the intensity of the preferences, represented by taking a positive power of all comparisons. Fourth, both the ranking position and the normalised weight of an object might change counter-intuitively after modifying a particular comparison. Fifth, the right eigenvector is not necessarily Pareto efficient: a dominating weight vector that approximates each pairwise comparison at least as well, with an improvement in at least one position, could exist. All violations of the theoretical properties are highlighted by illustrative examples. We also present several open questions in order to inspire future research.

</details>


### [6] [The Riemannian Landing Method: From projected gradient flows to SQP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24309)
*Florentin Goyens,Florian Feppon*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一的几何框架，揭示着陆方法在适当黎曼度量选择下包含多种经典优化方法，并分析着陆方法通过斜投影器参数化度量，为矩阵优化提供系统设计指南。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 着陆方法作为黎曼矩阵优化中处理非线性等式约束的有效方案，但缺乏统一的理论框架来理解其与经典优化方法的关系，以及如何系统设计度量以获得显式搜索方向。

Method: 提出一个统一的几何框架，通过黎曼度量的选择将着陆方法与经典优化方法联系起来；使用斜投影器场参数化度量，分析正交性、切向和法向度量的作用；为矩阵优化提供系统设计指南。

Result: 证明在适当度量选择下，着陆方法包含投影梯度流、零空间梯度流、SQP和增广拉格朗日方法；二次收敛着陆方法本质上重现二次收敛SQP方法；提出使用自适应步长的全局收敛着陆方法。

Conclusion: 着陆方法提供了一个统一的几何框架，连接多种经典优化方法；通过斜投影器参数化度量可以系统设计显式搜索方向；该框架不仅恢复现有正交约束问题的构造，还为设计新度量提供指导。

Abstract: Landing methods have recently emerged in Riemannian matrix optimization as efficient schemes for handling nonlinear equality constraints without resorting to costly retractions. These methods decompose the search direction into tangent and normal components, enabling asymptotic feasibility while maintaining inexpensive updates. In this work, we provide a unifying geometric framework which reveals that, under suitable choices of Riemannian metric, the landing algorithm encompasses several classical optimization methods such as projected and null-space gradient flows, Sequential Quadratic Programming (SQP), and a certain form of the augmented Lagrangian method. In particular, we show that a quadratically convergent landing method essentially reproduces the quadratically convergent SQP method. These connections also allow us to propose a globally convergent landing method using adaptive step sizes. The backtracking line search satisfies an Armijo condition on a merit function, and does not require prior knowledge of Lipschitz constants.
  Our second key contribution is to analyze landing methods through a geometric parameterization of the metric in terms of fields of oblique projectors and associated metric restrictions. This viewpoint disentangles the roles of orthogonality, tangent and normal metrics, and elucidates how to design the metric to obtain explicit tangent and normal updates. For matrix optimization, this framework not only recovers recent constructions in the literature for problems with orthogonality constraints, but also provides systematic guidelines for designing new metrics that admit closed-form search directions.

</details>


### [7] [A unified modeling framework and improved formulations for single-hoist cyclic scheduling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24316)
*Markó Horváth*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该论文重新审视循环吊车调度问题的建模，通过统一视角分析现有MIP模型，识别不一致性，提出CP基准模型和改进的MIP公式，并提供公开基准库支持可重复研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 循环吊车调度问题在电镀生产线中广泛应用，但文献中存在一个令人困惑的现象：不同研究对相同基准实例报告不同的最优周期时间，这限制了计算结果的比较性和可重复性。

Method: 1. 从统一视角重新审视循环吊车调度问题的建模；2. 分析文献中提出的多个混合整数线性规划（MIP）公式；3. 识别建模不一致性并澄清现有公式之间的关系；4. 提出简单的约束规划（CP）模型作为基准方法；5. 推导改进的MIP公式；6. 进行广泛的计算实验比较不同公式的强度和性能。

Result: 1. 识别了现有MIP模型中的建模不一致性；2. 澄清了不同公式之间的关系；3. 提出了可作为基准的CP模型；4. 推导了改进的MIP公式；5. 通过计算实验比较了不同公式的性能；6. 创建了包含基准实例和多种CP/MIP公式实现的公开库。

Conclusion: 该研究为循环吊车调度问题提供了统一的建模视角，解决了文献中结果不一致的问题，提出的CP基准模型和改进MIP公式为未来研究提供了可靠基础，公开库的建立支持了该领域的可重复研究。

Abstract: The cyclic hoist scheduling problem originates in electroplating lines, where a single or multiple hoists transport parts between processing tanks subject to technological constraints. The objective is typically to determine a cyclic sequence of hoist movements that minimizes the cycle time while satisfying travel and processing constraints. Although the problem has been widely studied for several decades, the literature contains a puzzling phenomenon: different studies often report different optimal cycle times for the same benchmark instances, which limits the comparability and reproducibility of computational results.
  In this paper, we revisit the modeling of cyclic hoist scheduling problems from a unified perspective. We introduce a consistent modeling approach for single-hoist problems and analyze several mixed-integer linear programming (MIP) formulations proposed in the literature. Our analysis identifies modeling inconsistencies and clarifies the relationships between existing formulations. Based on these observations, we propose straightforward constraint programming (CP) models that can serve as baseline approaches, and we also derive improved MIP~formulations. Extensive computational experiments compare the strength and performance of the investigated formulations.
  To support reproducible research, we also provide a publicly available library containing benchmark instances and implementations of several CP and MIP~formulations for single-hoist cyclic hoist scheduling.

</details>


### [8] [Adaptive decision-making for stochastic service network design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24369)
*Javier Duran Micco,Bilge Atasoy*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出一个结合元启发式、仿真和机器学习的两阶段优化框架，用于解决多式联运网络中考虑不确定旅行时间和有限卡车资源的服务网络设计问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物流服务提供商在多式联运网络中面临旅行时间不确定和卡车资源有限的挑战，需要同时处理战术决策（如运输请求接受、定期服务容量预订）和运营决策（如动态卡车分配、路径规划、应对中断的重新规划），传统方法难以有效处理这种复杂性和不确定性。

Method: 采用两阶段优化方法：1) 使用模拟退火元启发式算法解决战术问题；2) 通过离散事件仿真模型捕捉运营复杂性和不确定旅行时间的连锁效应，训练自适应代理模型支持决策；3) 将战术决策与运营决策集成，实现动态响应。

Result: 1) 在确定性版本问题上，模拟退火算法相比现有最优结果提高了解决方案质量并显著减少计算时间；2) 在随机问题上，基于学习的模拟退火相比完整仿真评估的基准算法，在目标函数值仅差5%的情况下，计算时间减少高达20倍。

Conclusion: 提出的算法在解决复杂服务网络设计问题上表现优异，证明了集成多种建模和优化技术的有效性，展示了此类方法在高效解决货运运输规划挑战方面的潜力。

Abstract: This paper addresses the Service Network Design (SND) problem for a logistics service provider (LSP) operating in a multimodal freight transport network, considering uncertain travel times and limited truck fleet availability. A two-stage optimization approach is proposed, which combines metaheuristics, simulation and machine learning components. This solution framework integrates tactical decisions, such as transport request acceptance and capacity booking for scheduled services, with operational decisions, including dynamic truck allocation, routing, and re-planning in response to disruptions. A simulated annealing (SA) metaheuristic is employed to solve the tactical problem, supported by an adaptive surrogate model trained using a discrete-event simulation model that captures operational complexities and cascading effects of uncertain travel times. The performance of the proposed method is evaluated using benchmark instances. First, the SA is tested on a deterministic version of the problem and compared to state-of-the-art results, demonstrating it can improve the solution quality and significantly reduce the computational time. Then, the proposed SA is applied to the more complex stochastic problem. Compared to a benchmark algorithm that executes a full simulation for each solution evaluation, the learning-based SA generates high quality solutions while significantly reducing computational effort, achieving only a 5% difference in objective function value while cutting computation time by up to 20 times. These results demonstrate the strong performance of the proposed algorithm in solving complex versions of the SND. Moreover, they highlight the effectiveness of integrating diverse modeling and optimization techniques, and the potential of such approaches to efficiently address freight transport planning challenges.

</details>


### [9] [Optimal local interventions in the two-dimensional Abelian sandpile model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24459)
*Maike C. de Jongh,Richard J. Boucherie,M. N. M. van Lieshout*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 论文对阿贝尔沙堆模型中的雪崩规模控制策略进行了首次严格分析，研究通过移除特定位置沙粒来减少雪崩规模的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阿贝尔沙堆模型是自组织临界性的典型例子，其大规模雪崩事件可类比地震、森林火灾等灾难现象。研究旨在探索减少这些雪崩规模的控制策略。

Method: 开发并形式化了一种扩展方法来计算源自临界顶点连通分量的雪崩预期规模；特别分析了正方形分量中的干预效果；研究了外部控制器通过移除选定位置沙粒来扰动配置的干预策略。

Result: 最优干预位置需要在减少最大雪崩规模和增加缓解雪崩数量之间取得平衡；对正方形分量中的干预效果进行了显式分析；揭示了雪崩结构的特征。

Conclusion: 首次对阿贝尔沙堆模型中的干预影响进行了严格分析，为理解自组织临界系统中灾难性事件的缓解策略提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The Abelian sandpile model serves as a canonical example of self-organized criticality. This critical behavior manifests itself through large cascading events triggered by small perturbations. Such large-scale events, known as avalanches, are often regarded as stylized representations of catastrophic phenomena, such as earthquakes or forest fires. Motivated by this perspective, we study strategies to reduce avalanche sizes. We provide a first rigorous analysis of the impact of interventions in the Abelian sandpile model, considering a setting in which an external controller can perturb a configuration by removing sand grains at selected locations. We first develop and formalize an extended method to compute the expected size of an avalanche originating from a connected component of critical vertices, i.e., vertices at maximum height. Using this method, we characterize the structure of avalanches starting from square components and explicitly analyze the effect of interventions in such components. Our results show that the optimal intervention locations strike an interesting balance between reduction of largest avalanche sizes and increasing the number of mitigated avalanches.

</details>


### [10] [Model Predictive Path Integral Control as Preconditioned Gradient Descent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24489)
*Mahyar Fazlyab,Sina Sharifi,Jiarui Wang*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: MPPI控制是一种基于采样的轨迹优化方法，本文从变分优化理论角度重新解释MPPI，将其视为KL正则化分布优化问题，并推导出收敛性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MPPI控制虽然在非线性非凸环境中广泛应用，但其优化结构尚未被充分理解。作者希望通过变分优化理论视角，为MPPI提供更严格的数学解释和收敛性分析。

Method: 将约束轨迹优化问题提升为KL正则化的分布优化问题，转化为负对数配分函数（自由能）目标。对于一般参数族，得到分布参数的预条件梯度方法；对于固定协方差高斯族，证明经典MPPI等价于单位步长的预条件梯度下降。

Result: 建立了MPPI的变分优化理论解释，推导出收敛性分析：在有界可行集下，给出了光滑常数的显式上界和保证精确MPPI下降的充分条件。数值实验验证了理论并展示了关键超参数对性能的影响。

Conclusion: 本文为MPPI控制提供了严格的优化理论框架，揭示了其作为预条件梯度方法的本质，并建立了收敛性保证，为超参数选择和算法改进提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Model Predictive Path Integral (MPPI) control is a popular sampling-based method for trajectory optimization in nonlinear and nonconvex settings, yet its optimization structure remains only partially understood. We develop a variational, optimization-theoretic interpretation of MPPI by lifting constrained trajectory optimization to a KL-regularized problem over distributions and reducing it to a negative log-partition (free-energy) objective over a tractable sampling family. For a general parametric family, this yields a preconditioned gradient method on the distribution parameters and a natural multi-step extension of MPPI. For the fixed-covariance Gaussian family, we show that classical MPPI is recovered exactly as a preconditioned gradient descent step with unit step size. This interpretation enables a direct convergence analysis: under bounded feasible sets, we derive an explicit upper bound on the smoothness constant and a simple sufficient condition guaranteeing descent of exact MPPI. Numerical experiments support the theory and illustrate the effect of key hyperparameters on performance.

</details>


### [11] [Optimal control of infinite-dimensional dissipative systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24507)
*Anthony Hastir,Timo Reis*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 将无限维耗散系统的线性二次最优控制问题（可能含不定代价函数）转化为非负代价函数的等价问题


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究无限维耗散系统的不定线性二次最优控制问题，这类问题在控制理论中具有重要理论意义，但传统方法难以处理不定代价函数的情况

Method: 利用存储函数的存在性假设，将原不定最优控制问题转化为等价的非负代价函数线性二次最优控制问题，建立相应值函数关系，并推导算子Lur'e方程

Result: 证明了在存储函数存在条件下，不定最优控制问题可等价转化为非负代价函数问题，建立了值函数之间的明确关系，给出了算子Lur'e方程

Conclusion: 通过存储函数方法成功处理了无限维耗散系统的不定线性二次最优控制问题，为这类复杂控制问题的求解提供了有效理论框架

Abstract: We study the linear-quadratic optimal control problem for infinite-dimensional dissipative systems with possibly indefinite cost functional. Under the assumption that a storage function exists, we show that this indefinite optimal control problem is equivalent to a linear-quadratic optimal control problem with a nonnegative cost functional. We establish the relationship between the corresponding value functions and present the associated operator Lur'e equation. Finally, we illustrate our results with several examples.

</details>

### [12] [PDGMM-VAE: A Variational Autoencoder with Adaptive Per-Dimension Gaussian Mixture Model Priors for Nonlinear ICA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23547)
*Yuan-Hao Wei,Yan-Jie Sun*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: PDGMM-VAE：一种源导向的变分自编码器，为每个潜在维度（解释为独立源信号）分配独立的GMM先验，通过自适应学习先验参数实现盲源分离


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统VAE使用共享简单先验无法有效捕获源信号的非高斯统计特性，限制了盲源分离性能。需要为不同源信号设计异质先验以更好地促进分离

Method: 提出PDGMM-VAE框架，每个潜在维度（对应一个源信号）分配独立的GMM先验，先验参数与编码器-解码器参数一起端到端自适应学习。编码器作为解混映射，解码器从推断分量重建观测混合

Result: 在线性和非线性混合问题上，PDGMM-VAE能够有效恢复潜在源信号并取得满意的分离性能

Conclusion: 通过为不同潜在源配备不同GMM先验的VAE框架，实现了端到端训练和先验自适应学习，为盲源分离提供了一种系统化的概率方法

Abstract: Independent component analysis is a core framework within blind source separation for recovering latent source signals from observed mixtures under statistical independence assumptions. In this work, we propose PDGMM-VAE, a source-oriented variational autoencoder in which each latent dimension, interpreted explicitly as an individual source signal, is assigned its own Gaussian mixture model prior. Unlike conventional VAE formulations with a shared simple prior, the proposed framework imposes per-dimension heterogeneous prior constraints, enabling the model to capture diverse non-Gaussian source statistics and thereby promote source separation under a probabilistic encoder-decoder architecture. Importantly, the parameters of these per-dimension GMM priors are not fixed in advance, but are adaptively learned and automatically refined toward convergence together with the encoder and decoder parameters under the overall training objective. Within this formulation, the encoder serves as a demixing mapping from observations to latent sources, while the decoder reconstructs the observed mixtures from the inferred components. The proposed model provides a systematic study of an idea that had previously only been noted in our preliminary form, namely, equipping different latent sources with different GMM priors for ICA, and formulates it as a full VAE framework with end-to-end training and per-dimension prior learning. Experimental results on both linear and nonlinear mixing problems demonstrate that PDGMM-VAE can recover latent source signals and achieve satisfactory separation performance.

### [13] [The Mass Agreement Score: A Point-centric Measure of Cluster Size Consistency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23581)
*Randolph Wiredu-Aidoo*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 提出Mass Agreement Score (MAS)作为聚类均匀性度量，解决传统基于标签的度量在标签数量扰动下的不稳定性问题


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚类中某个簇的规模过大通常是不理想的，需要一种能衡量簇大小均匀性的度量来筛选此类划分。传统基于标签的度量在标签数量变化时不稳定，因为算法可能产生不同数量的标签，即使底层点分布变化很小

Method: 引入Mass Agreement Score (MAS)，这是一种点中心的度量，范围在[0,1]之间。它从每个簇中点的视角评估期望簇大小的一致性。通过设计实现片段鲁棒性，对具有相似主体结构的划分给出相似分数，同时对簇质量的真实重新分布保持敏感

Result: MAS度量具有稳定性：在点分配只有微小差异的划分会获得相似的均匀性分数。它能够抵抗标签数量扰动，因为不直接依赖于标签本身

Conclusion: MAS提供了一种鲁棒的聚类均匀性度量方法，解决了传统基于标签的度量在标签数量变化时的不稳定性问题，为评估聚类质量提供了更可靠的工具

Abstract: In clustering, strong dominance in the size of a particular cluster is often undesirable, motivating a measure of cluster size uniformity that can be used to filter such partitions. A basic requirement of such a measure is stability: partitions that differ only slightly in their point assignments should receive similar uniformity scores. A difficulty arises because cluster labels are not fixed objects; algorithms may produce different numbers of labels even when the underlying point distribution changes very little. Measures defined directly over labels can therefore become unstable under label-count perturbations. I introduce the Mass Agreement Score (MAS), a point-centric metric bounded in [0, 1] that evaluates the consistency of expected cluster size as measured from the perspective of points in each cluster. Its construction yields fragment robustness by design, assigning similar scores to partitions with similar bulk structure while remaining sensitive to genuine redistribution of cluster mass.

</details>


### [14] [Wasserstein Parallel Transport for Predicting the Dynamics of Statistical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23736)
*Tristan Luca Saidi,Gonzalo Mena,Larry Wasserman,Florian Gunsilius*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 论文提出"Wasserstein Parallel Trends"方法，通过最优传输测地线的平行输运来比较分布动态，解决因果推断、领域适应和反事实预测中的分布演化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多科学系统（如细胞群体或经济队列）自然地被描述为随时间演化的概率分布。预测系统在不同力量或初始条件下如何演化对因果推断、领域适应和反事实预测至关重要。然而，分布空间通常缺乏经典方法所依赖的向量空间结构。

Method: 引入分布层面的平行动态概念，基于最优传输测地线的切向动态平行输运。提出Wasserstein流形上的新型扇形方案，能高效近似测地线平行输运，并为Wasserstein空间中的平行输运提供首个理论保证。推导出高斯测度的闭式平行输运。

Result: Wasserstein Parallel Trends方法能恢复经典平行趋势假设（针对平均值）作为特例。在合成数据和两个单细胞RNA测序数据集上成功应用，用于跨生物系统的基因表达动态插补。

Conclusion: 通过用测地线平行输运替代经典方法的向量减法，该方法能在因果推断、领域适应和实验设置中的批次效应校正等应用中提供分布动态的反事实比较，为分布演化分析提供了理论基础和实用工具。

Abstract: Many scientific systems, such as cellular populations or economic cohorts, are naturally described by probability distributions that evolve over time. Predicting how such a system would have evolved under different forces or initial conditions is fundamental to causal inference, domain adaptation, and counterfactual prediction. However, the space of distributions often lacks the vector space structure on which classical methods rely. To address this, we introduce a general notion of parallel dynamics at a distributional level. We base this principle on parallel transport of tangent dynamics along optimal transport geodesics and call it ``Wasserstein Parallel Trends''. By replacing the vector subtraction of classic methods with geodesic parallel transport, we can provide counterfactual comparisons of distributional dynamics in applications such as causal inference, domain adaptation, and batch-effect correction in experimental settings. The main mathematical contribution is a novel notion of fanning scheme on the Wasserstein manifold that allows us to efficiently approximate parallel transport along geodesics while also providing the first theoretical guarantees for parallel transport in the Wasserstein space. We also show that Wasserstein Parallel Trends recovers the classic parallel trends assumption for averages as a special case and derive closed-form parallel transport for Gaussian measures. We deploy the method on synthetic data and two single-cell RNA sequencing datasets to impute gene-expression dynamics across biological systems.

</details>


### [15] [Beyond Consistency: Inference for the Relative risk functional in Deep Nonparametric Cox Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23835)
*Sattwik Ghosal,Xuran Meng,Yi Li*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 该论文建立了深度Cox比例风险模型估计量的渐近分布理论，解决了优化误差传播、点偏倚控制和集成不确定性量化等理论问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度神经网络在非参数Cox比例风险模型中存在理论空白：梯度优化误差如何影响总体风险、点偏倚如何控制以进行有效推断、集成不确定性量化在现实方差衰减机制下的行为。

Method: 1) 建立一般训练网络的非渐近oracle不等式，连接样本内优化误差与总体风险；2) 构建结构化神经参数化，实现与oracle界兼容的无穷范数逼近率；3) 在Hajek-Hoeffding投影下证明子采样集成估计量的点态和多变量渐近正态性；4) 推导平衡偏倚校正与投影主导性的子采样规模范围；5) 使用无穷小刀切法进行协方差估计和Wald型推断。

Result: 1) 建立了深度Cox估计量的渐近分布理论；2) 获得了点态和多变量渐近正态性结果；3) 推导了满足单重叠协方差衰减条件的子采样规模范围；4) 实现了相对风险对比(如对数风险比)的有效Wald型推断；5) 通过模拟和实际数据应用验证了理论。

Conclusion: 该研究填补了深度Cox模型的理论空白，提供了优化误差传播、偏倚控制和集成不确定性量化的完整理论框架，支持有效的统计推断。

Abstract: There remain theoretical gaps in deep neural network estimators for the nonparametric Cox proportional hazards model. In particular, it is unclear how gradient-based optimization error propagates to population risk under partial likelihood, how pointwise bias can be controlled to permit valid inference, and how ensemble-based uncertainty quantification behaves under realistic variance decay regimes. We develop an asymptotic distribution theory for deep Cox estimators that addresses these issues. First, we establish nonasymptotic oracle inequalities for general trained networks that link in-sample optimization error to population risk without requiring the exact empirical risk optimizer. We then construct a structured neural parameterization that achieves infinity-norm approximation rates compatible with the oracle bound, yielding control of the pointwise bias. Under these conditions and using the Hajek--Hoeffding projection, we prove pointwise and multivariate asymptotic normality for subsampled ensemble estimators. We derive a range of subsample sizes that balances bias correction with the requirement that the Hajek--Hoeffding projection remain dominant. This range accommodates decay conditions on the single-overlap covariance, which measures how strongly a single shared observation influences the estimator, and is weaker than those imposed in the subsampling literature. An infinitesimal jackknife representation provides analytic covariance estimation and valid Wald-type inference for relative risk contrasts such as log-hazard ratios. Finally, we illustrate the finite-sample implications of the theory through simulations and a real data application.

</details>

*Bowen Lu,Liangqiang Yang,Teng Li*

Main category: stat.ML

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图神经网络在图相关任务中表现出色，但在分布外数据上泛化能力差，因为它们倾向于学习虚假相关性。这些虚假相关性导致GNN在OOD设置下无法稳定学习预测表示与真实标签之间的互信息。

Method: 1. 从节点分类的本质出发构建因果图，采用后门调整阻断非因果路径，理论上推导出提高GNN OOD泛化能力的下界；2. 提出结合因果表示学习和损失替换策略的新方法：前者捕获节点级因果不变性并重建图后验分布，后者引入同阶渐近损失替换原始损失。

Abstract: Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) have achieved impressive performance in graph-related tasks. However, they suffer from poor generalization on out-of-distribution (OOD) data, as they tend to learn spurious correlations. Such correlations present a phenomenon that GNNs fail to stably learn the mutual information between prediction representations and ground-truth labels under OOD settings. To address these challenges, we formulate a causal graph starting from the essence of node classification, adopt backdoor adjustment to block non-causal paths, and theoretically derive a lower bound for improving OOD generalization of GNNs. To materialize these insights, we further propose a novel approach integrating causal representation learning and a loss replacement strategy. The former captures node-level causal invariance and reconstructs graph posterior distribution. The latter introduces asymptotic losses of the same order to replace the original losses. Extensive experiments demonstrate the superiority of our method in OOD generalization and effectively alleviating the phenomenon of unstable mutual information learning.

Abstract: Privacy and algorithmic fairness have become two central issues in modern machine learning. In this paper, we systematically study the joint impact of differential privacy and fairness on classification in a federated setting, where data are distributed across multiple servers. Targeting demographic disparity constrained classification under federated differential privacy, we propose a two-step algorithm, namely FDP-Fair. In the special case where there is only one server, we further propose a simple yet powerful algorithm, namely CDP-Fair, serving as a computationally-lightweight alternative. Under mild structural assumptions, theoretical guarantees on privacy, fairness and excess risk control are established. In particular, we disentangle the source of the private fairness-aware excess risk into a) intrinsic cost of classification, b) cost of private classification, c) non-private cost of fairness and d) private cost of fairness. Our theoretical findings are complemented by extensive numerical experiments on both synthetic and real datasets, highlighting the practicality of our designed algorithms.

### [19] [Continuous-Time Learning of Probability Distributions: A Case Study in a Digital Trial of Young Children with Type 1 Diabetes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24427)
*Antonio Álvarez-López,Marcos Matabuena*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 提出一个概率框架，使用神经ODE建模葡萄糖分布的连续时间演化，通过高斯混合模型表示分布，时间变化的混合权重由神经ODE控制，使用最大平均差异进行参数估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在糖尿病监测中，理解生物标志物分布随时间演变是核心挑战。传统汇总指标会遗漏疾病进展和治疗反应的分布模式变化。受一项26周临床试验的启发，该试验比较了闭环胰岛素输送系统t:slim X2与标准疗法在儿童1型糖尿病中的效果。

Method: 使用高斯混合模型表示葡萄糖分布，混合权重随时间变化并由神经ODE控制。采用基于最大平均差异的分布匹配准则进行参数估计，构建可解释、计算高效的概率框架。

Result: 该方法能够检测到传统分析方法难以捕捉的治疗相关葡萄糖动态改善，对细微的时间分布变化敏感，成功应用于连续葡萄糖监测试验数据。

Conclusion: 提出的概率框架能够有效建模时间索引分布的连续时间演化，在糖尿病监测中提供了比传统方法更敏感的分布变化检测能力，有助于揭示疾病进展和治疗反应的模式。

Abstract: Understanding how biomarker distributions evolve over time is a central challenge in digital health and chronic disease monitoring. In diabetes, changes in the distribution of glucose measurements can reveal patterns of disease progression and treatment response that conventional summary measures miss. Motivated by a 26-week clinical trial comparing the closed-loop insulin delivery system t:slim X2 with standard therapy in children with type 1 diabetes, we propose a probabilistic framework to model the continuous-time evolution of time-indexed distributions using continuous glucose monitoring data (CGM) collected every five minutes. We represent the glucose distribution as a Gaussian mixture, with time-varying mixture weights governed by a neural ODE. We estimate the model parameter using a distribution-matching criterion based on the maximum mean discrepancy. The resulting framework is interpretable, computationally efficient, and sensitive to subtle temporal distributional changes. Applied to CGM trial data, the method detects treatment-related improvements in glucose dynamics that are difficult to capture with traditional analytical approaches.

</details>


### [20] [Trust Region Constrained Bayesian Optimization with Penalized Constraint Handling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24567)
*Raju Chowdhury,Tanmay Sen,Prajamitra Bhuyan,Biswabrata Pradhan*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 提出一种结合惩罚函数、代理模型和信赖域策略的贝叶斯优化方法，用于解决高维黑盒约束优化问题，在减少评估次数的同时获得高质量可行解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维黑盒约束优化面临评估成本高、缺乏梯度信息、可行域复杂等挑战，需要开发高效且稳定的优化方法。

Method: 将约束问题通过惩罚函数转换为无约束形式，结合信赖域策略限制搜索范围，在局部区域内使用代理模型和期望改进采集函数进行点选择。

Result: 在合成和真实世界的高维约束优化问题上，该方法相比现有方法能用更少评估次数识别高质量可行解，且在不同设置下保持稳定性能。

Conclusion: 提出的信赖域方法通过整合惩罚约束处理和局部代理建模，实现了对可行域的高效探索，同时保持了样本效率，为高维黑盒约束优化提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Constrained optimization in high-dimensional black-box settings is difficult due to expensive evaluations, the lack of gradient information, and complex feasibility regions. In this work, we propose a Bayesian optimization method that combines a penalty formulation, a surrogate model, and a trust region strategy. The constrained problem is converted to an unconstrained form by penalizing constraint violations, which provides a unified modeling framework. A trust region restricts the search to a local region around the current best solution, which improves stability and efficiency in high dimensions. Within this region, we use the Expected Improvement acquisition function to select evaluation points by balancing improvement and uncertainty. The proposed Trust Region method integrates penalty-based constraint handling with local surrogate modeling. This combination enables efficient exploration of feasible regions while maintaining sample efficiency. We compare the proposed method with state-of-the-art methods on synthetic and real-world high-dimensional constrained optimization problems. The results show that the method identifies high-quality feasible solutions with fewer evaluations and maintains stable performance across different settings.

</details>

### [21] [PLDR-LLMs Reason At Self-Organized Criticality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23539)
*Burc Gokden*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PLDR-LLMs在自组织临界状态下训练时，在推理时表现出推理能力，其演绎输出特性类似于二阶相变，可通过序参量量化推理能力


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究大型语言模型中推理能力如何产生，提供不依赖基准数据集评估的量化方法，从模型参数本身解释推理能力的涌现

Method: 在自组织临界状态下预训练PLDR-LLMs，分析演绎输出参数，定义序参量，比较临界和亚临界状态下的模型性能

Result: 临界状态下模型演绎输出达到亚稳态，学习到标度函数、普适类和重整化群等表示，序参量接近零时推理能力最佳，基准测试支持这一观察

Conclusion: PLDR-LLMs在临界状态下获得推理能力，可通过演绎输出参数的全局统计定义序参量来量化推理能力，无需依赖归纳输出的基准数据集评估

Abstract: We show that PLDR-LLMs pretrained at self-organized criticality exhibit reasoning at inference time. The characteristics of PLDR-LLM deductive outputs at criticality is similar to second-order phase transitions. At criticality, the correlation length diverges, and the deductive outputs attain a metastable steady state. The steady state behaviour suggests that deductive outputs learn representations equivalent to scaling functions, universality classes and renormalization groups from the training dataset, leading to generalization and reasoning capabilities in the process. We can then define an order parameter from the global statistics of the model's deductive output parameters at inference. The reasoning capabilities of a PLDR-LLM is better when its order parameter is close to zero at criticality. This observation is supported by the benchmark scores of the models trained at near-criticality and sub-criticality. Our results provide a self-contained explanation on how reasoning manifests in large language models, and the ability to reason can be quantified solely from global model parameter values of the deductive outputs at steady state, without any need for evaluation of curated benchmark datasets through inductive output for reasoning and comprehension.

</details>


### [22] [Environment Maps: Structured Environmental Representations for Long-Horizon Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23610)
*Yenchia Feng,Chirag Sharma,Karime Maamari*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出环境地图（Environment Maps）作为解决LLM在复杂软件工作流中长时程规划问题的持久化、与智能体无关的结构化表示方法，通过整合屏幕录制、执行轨迹等异构证据构建结构化图，显著提升任务成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型发展迅速，但在复杂软件工作流的鲁棒自动化方面仍存在挑战。在长时程设置中，智能体常因级联错误和环境随机性而失败，动态界面中的单个错误步骤就可能导致任务失败，产生幻觉或陷入试错循环。

Method: 提出环境地图框架，将异构证据（屏幕录制、执行轨迹等）整合为结构化图表示，包含四个核心组件：1) 上下文（抽象位置）；2) 动作（参数化可供性）；3) 工作流（观察到的轨迹）；4) 隐性知识（领域定义和可重用程序）。在WebArena基准测试的五个领域进行评估。

Result: 配备环境地图的智能体在WebArena基准测试中达到28.2%的成功率，几乎是仅使用会话绑定上下文基线（14.2%）的两倍，也优于直接访问用于生成环境地图的原始轨迹数据的智能体（23.3%）。

Conclusion: 环境地图通过在模型和环境之间提供结构化接口，为长时程规划建立了持久化基础，具有人类可解释、可编辑和可增量精炼的特性，显著提升了复杂软件工作流自动化的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Although large language models (LLMs) have advanced rapidly, robust automation of complex software workflows remains an open problem. In long-horizon settings, agents frequently suffer from cascading errors and environmental stochasticity; a single misstep in a dynamic interface can lead to task failure, resulting in hallucinations or trial-and-error. This paper introduces $\textit{Environment Maps}$: a persistent, agent-agnostic representation that mitigates these failures by consolidating heterogeneous evidence, such as screen recordings and execution traces, into a structured graph. The representation consists of four core components: (1) Contexts (abstracted locations), (2) Actions (parameterized affordances), (3) Workflows (observed trajectories), and (4) Tacit Knowledge (domain definitions and reusable procedures). We evaluate this framework on the WebArena benchmark across five domains. Agents equipped with environment maps achieve a 28.2% success rate, nearly doubling the performance of baselines limited to session-bound context (14.2%) and outperforming agents that have access to the raw trajectory data used to generate the environment maps (23.3%). By providing a structured interface between the model and the environment, Environment Maps establish a persistent foundation for long-horizon planning that is human-interpretable, editable, and incrementally refinable.

</details>


### [23] [Evaluating a Multi-Agent Voice-Enabled Smart Speaker for Care Homes: A Safety-Focused Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23625)
*Zeinab Dehghani,Rameez Raja Kureshi,Koorosh Aslansefat,Faezeh Alsadat Abedi,Dhavalkumar Thakker,Lisa Greaves,Bhupesh Kumar Mishra,Baseer Ahmad,Tanaya Maslekar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文评估了面向养老院的智能语音系统，该系统结合Whisper语音识别和RAG技术，用于支持日常护理活动。通过安全评估框架，在330个语音转录中测试了居民识别、提醒提取和日程安排准确性，最佳配置下居民ID和护理类别匹配达100%，提醒识别达89.09%，端到端日程安排准确率达84.65%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在健康和社会护理领域，人工智能被用于减少行政工作量，让工作人员有更多时间专注于患者护理。本研究旨在评估智能语音系统在养老院环境中的应用，特别关注安全性和可靠性，因为养老院是安全关键环境。

Method: 采用安全导向的端到端评估框架，结合Whisper语音识别与检索增强生成（RAG）方法（混合、稀疏和密集）。通过监督式养老院试验和受控测试，评估了330个语音转录，涵盖11个护理类别，包括184个包含提醒的交互。评估重点包括：居民和护理类别的正确识别、提醒识别和提取、以及不确定性下的端到端日程安排正确性（包括安全延迟/澄清）。特别关注嘈杂环境和多样口音的可靠性，采用置信度评分、澄清提示和人在环监督。

Result: 最佳配置（GPT-5.2）下：居民ID和护理类别匹配达到100%（95% CI: 98.86-100）；提醒识别达到89.09%（95% CI: 83.81-92.80），零漏检（100%召回率）但存在一些误报；通过日历集成的端到端日程安排达到84.65%的精确提醒计数一致性（95% CI: 78.00-89.56）。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，经过仔细评估并采取适当安全措施的语音系统，能够支持养老院环境中的准确文档记录、有效任务管理和可信赖的AI应用。系统在安全关键环境中表现出良好的性能，但仍存在将非正式口头指令转换为可操作事件的边缘情况。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence (AI) is increasingly being explored in health and social care to reduce administrative workload and allow staff to spend more time on patient care. This paper evaluates a voice-enabled Care Home Smart Speaker designed to support everyday activities in residential care homes, including spoken access to resident records, reminders, and scheduling tasks. A safety-focused evaluation framework is presented that examines the system end-to-end, combining Whisper-based speech recognition with retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) approaches (hybrid, sparse, and dense). Using supervised care-home trials and controlled testing, we evaluated 330 spoken transcripts across 11 care categories, including 184 reminder-containing interactions. These evaluations focus on (i) correct identification of residents and care categories, (ii) reminder recognition and extraction, and (iii) end-to-end scheduling correctness under uncertainty (including safe deferral/clarification). Given the safety-critical nature of care homes, particular attention is also paid to reliability in noisy environments and across diverse accents, supported by confidence scoring, clarification prompts, and human-in-the-loop oversight. In the best-performing configuration (GPT-5.2), resident ID and care category matching reached 100% (95% CI: 98.86-100), while reminder recognition reached 89.09\% (95% CI: 83.81-92.80) with zero missed reminders (100% recall) but some false positives. End-to-end scheduling via calendar integration achieved 84.65% exact reminder-count agreement (95% CI: 78.00-89.56), indicating remaining edge cases in converting informal spoken instructions into actionable events. The findings suggest that voice-enabled systems, when carefully evaluated and appropriately safeguarded, can support accurate documentation, effective task management, and trustworthy use of AI in care home settings.

### [24] [Can LLM Agents Be CFOs? A Benchmark for Resource Allocation in Dynamic Enterprise Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23638)
*Yi Han,Lingfei Qian,Yan Wang,Yueru He,Xueqing Peng,Dongji Feng,Yankai Chen,Haohang Li,Yupeng Cao,Jimin Huang,Xue Liu,Jian-Yun Nie,Sophia Ananiadou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: EnterpriseArena：首个评估LLM智能体在长期企业资源分配中表现的基准，模拟132个月的企业运营环境，结果显示当前LLM在此任务上存在显著能力差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LLM在推理、规划和执行复杂任务方面表现出色，但它们在不确定性下进行长期资源分配的能力尚不明确。资源分配需要长期承诺稀缺资源、平衡竞争目标并为未来需求保留灵活性，这与短期反应性决策有本质区别。

Method: 引入EnterpriseArena基准，模拟CFO风格的决策制定，包含132个月的企业模拟器，整合公司级财务数据、匿名商业文档、宏观经济和行业信号以及专家验证的运营规则。环境是部分可观测的，仅通过预算组织工具揭示状态，迫使智能体在信息获取和资源节约之间权衡。

Result: 对11个先进LLM的实验表明该设置极具挑战性：仅有16%的运行能完成整个时间跨度，更大的模型并不总是优于更小的模型。这揭示了当前LLM智能体在不确定性下的长期资源分配方面存在明显能力差距。

Conclusion: 长期资源分配在不确定性下是当前LLM智能体的一个独特能力缺口，需要专门的研究和开发来解决这一挑战。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have enabled agentic systems that can reason, plan, and act across complex tasks, but it remains unclear whether they can allocate resources effectively under uncertainty. Unlike short-horizon reactive decisions, allocation requires committing scarce resources over time while balancing competing objectives and preserving flexibility for future needs. We introduce EnterpriseArena, the first benchmark for evaluating agents on long-horizon enterprise resource allocation. It instantiates CFO-style decision-making in a 132-month enterprise simulator combining firm-level financial data, anonymized business documents, macroeconomic and industry signals, and expert-validated operating rules. The environment is partially observable and reveals the state only through budgeted organizational tools, forcing agents to trade off information acquisition against conserving scarce resources. Experiments on eleven advanced LLMs show that this setting remains highly challenging: only 16% of runs survive the full horizon, and larger models do not reliably outperform smaller ones. These results identify long-horizon resource allocation under uncertainty as a distinct capability gap for current LLM agents.

*Marc-Antoine Provost,Nejc Ilenic,Christopher Solinas,Philippe Beardsell*

TL;DR: GTO Wizard Benchmark是一个用于评估无限制德州扑克单挑算法的标准化框架，通过对抗近似纳什均衡的超级AI代理，并采用方差减少技术提高评估效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发公开API和标准化评估框架，使用GTO Wizard AI（近似纳什均衡的超级扑克代理）作为基准对手，集成AIVAT方差减少技术，对主流大语言模型进行零样本基准测试。

Result: GTO Wizard AI以19.4±4.1 bb/100的优势击败前最强公开基准Slumbot；AIVAT技术将评估所需手数减少10倍；所有测试的LLM（包括GPT-5.4、Claude Opus 4.6等）表现均远低于基准水平。

Conclusion: 该基准为研究者在部分可观测多智能体系统中评估规划和推理进展提供了精确量化环境，尽管LLM近年有显著进步，但在扑克推理方面仍有巨大改进空间，特别是在表示和隐藏状态推理能力方面。

Abstract: We introduce GTO Wizard Benchmark, a public API and standardized evaluation framework for benchmarking algorithms in Heads-Up No-Limit Texas Hold'em (HUNL). The benchmark evaluates agents against GTO Wizard AI, a state-of-the-art superhuman poker agent that approximates Nash Equilibria, and defeated Slumbot, the 2018 Annual Computer Poker Competition champion and previous strongest publicly accessible HUNL benchmark, by $19.4$ $\pm$ $4.1$ bb/100. Variance is a fundamental challenge in poker evaluation; we address this by integrating AIVAT, a provably unbiased variance reduction technique that achieves equivalent statistical significance with ten times fewer hands than naive Monte Carlo evaluation. We conduct a comprehensive benchmarking study of state-of-the-art large language models under zero-shot conditions, including GPT-5.4, Claude Opus 4.6, Gemini 3.1 Pro, Grok 4, and others. Initial results and analysis reveal dramatic progress in LLM reasoning over recent years, yet all models remain far below the baseline established by our benchmark. Qualitative analysis reveals clear opportunities for improvement, including representation and the ability to reason over hidden states. This benchmark provides researchers with a precise and quantifiable setting to evaluate advances in planning and reasoning in multi-agent systems with partial observability.

### [26] [Grounding Vision and Language to 3D Masks for Long-Horizon Box Rearrangement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23676)
*Ashish Malik,Caleb Lowe,Aayam Shrestha,Stefan Lee,Fuxin Li,Alan Fern*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RAMP-3D：基于3D视觉语言模型的反应式掩码规划器，通过预测配对3D掩码（抓取对象掩码和放置区域掩码）解决3D盒子重排任务的长时程规划问题


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法（符号规划器和2D视觉语言模型）在处理多物体、复杂3D几何和隐式语义约束的3D环境规划任务时存在局限性，而3D视觉语言模型在自然语言指称到3D分割掩码的强基础能力为更通用的规划提供了可能

Method: 扩展现有3D基础模型，提出RAMP-3D（反应式动作掩码规划器），将长时程规划形式化为顺序反应式预测配对3D掩码：指示抓取对象的"which-object"掩码和指定放置区域的"which-target-region"掩码，系统处理RGB-D观测和自然语言任务规范，反应式生成多步抓取-放置动作

Result: 在包含1-30个盒子的仓库式环境中11个任务变体上进行实验，RAMP-3D在长时程重排任务上达到79.5%的成功率，显著优于基于2D视觉语言模型的基线方法

Conclusion: 基于掩码的反应式策略是长时程规划中符号管道的有前景的替代方案，RAMP-3D展示了3D视觉语言模型在复杂3D环境规划任务中的潜力

Abstract: We study long-horizon planning in 3D environments from under-specified natural-language goals using only visual observations, focusing on multi-step 3D box rearrangement tasks. Existing approaches typically rely on symbolic planners with brittle relational grounding of states and goals, or on direct action-sequence generation from 2D vision-language models (VLMs). Both approaches struggle with reasoning over many objects, rich 3D geometry, and implicit semantic constraints. Recent advances in 3D VLMs demonstrate strong grounding of natural-language referents to 3D segmentation masks, suggesting the potential for more general planning capabilities. We extend existing 3D grounding models and propose Reactive Action Mask Planner (RAMP-3D), which formulates long-horizon planning as sequential reactive prediction of paired 3D masks: a "which-object" mask indicating what to pick and a "which-target-region" mask specifying where to place it. The resulting system processes RGB-D observations and natural-language task specifications to reactively generate multi-step pick-and-place actions for 3D box rearrangement. We conduct experiments across 11 task variants in warehouse-style environments with 1-30 boxes and diverse natural-language constraints. RAMP-3D achieves 79.5% success rate on long-horizon rearrangement tasks and significantly outperforms 2D VLM-based baselines, establishing mask-based reactive policies as a promising alternative to symbolic pipelines for long-horizon planning.

</details>


### [27] [LLMs Do Not Grade Essays Like Humans](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23714)
*Jerin George Mathew,Sumayya Taher,Anindita Kundu,Denilson Barbosa*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估大型语言模型在自动作文评分中的表现，特别是在无需任务特定训练的情况下，LLM生成的分数与人类评分的一致性程度，以及LLM评分行为的特征。

Method: 在零样本设置下评估GPT和Llama系列模型，比较LLM生成的作文分数与人类评分，分析评分差异与作文特征（如长度、语法错误等）的关系，并考察LLM评分与反馈的一致性。

Result: LLM与人类评分者的一致性相对较弱且受作文特征影响：LLM倾向于给短篇或不完整作文更高分数，给包含轻微语法/拼写错误的长篇作文更低分数；LLM生成的评分与反馈具有一致性（更多表扬对应更高分数，更多批评对应更低分数）。

Conclusion: LLM生成的评分和反馈遵循一致的模式，但使用的信号与人类评分者不同，导致与人类评分实践的对齐有限；尽管如此，LLM可以可靠地用于支持作文评分，因为其反馈与评分具有一致性。

Abstract: Large language models have recently been proposed as tools for automated essay scoring, but their agreement with human grading remains unclear. In this work, we evaluate how LLM-generated scores compare with human grades and analyze the grading behavior of several models from the GPT and Llama families in an out-of-the-box setting, without task-specific training. Our results show that agreement between LLM and human scores remains relatively weak and varies with essay characteristics. In particular, compared to human raters, LLMs tend to assign higher scores to short or underdeveloped essays, while assigning lower scores to longer essays that contain minor grammatical or spelling errors. We also find that the scores generated by LLMs are generally consistent with the feedback they generate: essays receiving more praise tend to receive higher scores, while essays receiving more criticism tend to receive lower scores. These results suggest that LLM-generated scores and feedback follow coherent patterns but rely on signals that differ from those used by human raters, resulting in limited alignment with human grading practices. Nevertheless, our work shows that LLMs produce feedback that is consistent with their grading and that they can be reliably used in supporting essay scoring.

</details>


### [28] [Efficient Benchmarking of AI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23749)
*Franck Ndzomga*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究发现通过筛选中等难度任务（通过率30-70%）可大幅减少AI智能体评估成本（减少44-70%），同时保持排名可靠性，优于随机采样和贪婪选择


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI智能体评估成本高昂，需要交互式工具使用和多步推理。研究旨在探索是否可以通过小规模任务子集以显著降低成本来保持智能体排名可靠性

Method: 提出无需优化的简单协议：仅评估中等历史通过率（30-70%）的任务。该方法基于项目反应理论，在8个基准、33个智能体框架和70+模型配置上进行验证

Result: 研究发现绝对分数预测在框架驱动的分布偏移下会退化，但排名顺序预测保持稳定。中等难度任务筛选方法在框架和时间偏移下均能保持高排名保真度

Conclusion: 可靠的排行榜排名不需要完整基准评估，通过中等难度任务筛选可大幅降低评估成本，同时保持排名可靠性，优于随机采样和贪婪任务选择

Abstract: Evaluating AI agents on comprehensive benchmarks is expensive because each evaluation requires interactive rollouts with tool use and multi-step reasoning. We study whether small task subsets can preserve agent rankings at substantially lower cost. Unlike static language model benchmarks, agent evaluation is subject to scaffold-driven distribution shift, since performance depends on the framework wrapping the underlying model. Across eight benchmarks, 33 agent scaffolds, and 70+ model configurations, we find that absolute score prediction degrades under this shift, while rank-order prediction remains stable. Exploiting this asymmetry, we propose a simple optimization-free protocol: evaluate new agents only on tasks with intermediate historical pass rates (30-70%). This mid-range difficulty filter, motivated by Item Response Theory, reduces the number of evaluation tasks by 44-70% while maintaining high rank fidelity under scaffold and temporal shifts. It provides more reliable rankings than random sampling, which exhibits high variance across seeds, and outperforms greedy task selection under distribution shift. These results suggest that reliable leaderboard ranking does not require full-benchmark evaluation.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 终身多智能体路径规划对现代仓库自动化至关重要，但传统基于搜索的求解器需要昂贵调整，机器学习方法的优越性尚未明确，需要结合两者优势

Method: 提出RL-RH-PP框架，以经典优先规划为骨干，将动态优先级分配建模为POMDP，使用基于注意力的神经网络自回归解码优先级顺序，实现高效的顺序单智能体规划

Result: 在真实仓库模拟中，RL-RH-PP在基线方法中实现最高总吞吐量，能有效泛化到不同智能体密度、规划视野和仓库布局

Abstract: Lifelong Multi-Agent Path Finding (MAPF) is critical for modern warehouse automation, which requires multiple robots to continuously navigate conflict-free paths to optimize the overall system throughput. However, the complexity of warehouse environments and the long-term dynamics of lifelong MAPF often demand costly adaptations to classical search-based solvers. While machine learning methods have been explored, their superiority over search-based methods remains inconclusive. In this paper, we introduce Reinforcement Learning (RL) guided Rolling Horizon Prioritized Planning (RL-RH-PP), the first framework integrating RL with search-based planning for lifelong MAPF. Specifically, we leverage classical Prioritized Planning (PP) as a backbone for its simplicity and flexibility in integrating with a learning-based priority assignment policy. By formulating dynamic priority assignment as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP), RL-RH-PP exploits the sequential decision-making nature of lifelong planning while delegating complex spatial-temporal interactions among agents to reinforcement learning. An attention-based neural network autoregressively decodes priority orders on-the-fly, enabling efficient sequential single-agent planning by the PP planner. Evaluations in realistic warehouse simulations show that RL-RH-PP achieves the highest total throughput among baselines and generalizes effectively across agent densities, planning horizons, and warehouse layouts. Our interpretive analyses reveal that RL-RH-PP proactively prioritizes congested agents and strategically redirects agents from congestion, easing traffic flow and boosting throughput. These findings highlight the potential of learning-guided approaches to augment traditional heuristics in modern warehouse automation.

Abstract: With the growing demand for intelligent in-vehicle experiences, vehicle-based agents are evolving from simple assistants to long-term companions. This evolution requires agents to continuously model multi-user preferences and make reliable decisions in the face of inter-user preference conflicts and changing habits over time. However, existing benchmarks are largely limited to single-user, static question-answer settings, failing to capture the temporal evolution of preferences and the multi-user, tool-interactive nature of real vehicle environments. To address this gap, we introduce VehicleMemBench, a multi-user long-context memory benchmark built on an executable in-vehicle simulation environment. The benchmark evaluates tool use and memory by comparing the post-action environment state with a predefined target state, enabling objective and reproducible evaluation without LLM-based or human scoring. VehicleMemBench includes 23 tool modules, and each sample contains over 80 historical memory events. Experiments show that powerful models perform well on direct instruction tasks but struggle in scenarios involving memory evolution, particularly when user preferences change dynamically. Even advanced memory systems struggle to handle domain-specific memory requirements in this environment. These findings highlight the need for more robust and specialized memory management mechanisms to support long-term adaptive decision-making in real-world in-vehicle systems. To facilitate future research, we release the data and code.

### [31] [SCoOP: Semantic Consistent Opinion Pooling for Uncertainty Quantification in Multiple Vision-Language Model Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23853)
*Chung-En Johnny Yu,Brian Jalaian,Nathaniel D. Bastian*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SCoOP是一个无需训练的、基于语义一致意见池化的不确定性量化框架，用于多视觉语言模型系统，通过不确定性加权线性意见池化来检测幻觉和实现弃权决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 结合多个视觉语言模型可以增强多模态推理和鲁棒性，但聚合异构模型的输出会放大不确定性并增加幻觉风险。现有不确定性量化方法主要针对单一模型设计，缺乏对多模型系统级集体不确定性的有效度量。

Method: 提出SCoOP（语义一致意见池化）框架，通过不确定性加权线性意见池化来量化多VLM系统的不确定性。该方法无需训练，能够显式测量多个VLMs之间的集体系统级不确定性，支持有效的幻觉检测和不确定样本的弃权决策。

Result: 在ScienceQA数据集上，SCoOP在幻觉检测方面达到0.866的AUROC，比基线方法（0.732-0.757）提升约10-13%；在弃权决策方面达到0.907的AURAC，比基线（0.818-0.840）提升7-9%。该方法仅引入微秒级的聚合开销，相对于VLM推理时间（秒级）可忽略不计。

Conclusion: SCoOP为多视觉语言模型系统提供了一种高效且原理明确的不确定性感知聚合机制，显著提升了多模态AI系统的可靠性，同时保持了计算效率。

Abstract: Combining multiple Vision-Language Models (VLMs) can enhance multimodal reasoning and robustness, but aggregating heterogeneous models' outputs amplifies uncertainty and increases the risk of hallucinations. We propose SCoOP (Semantic-Consistent Opinion Pooling), a training-free uncertainty quantification (UQ) framework multi-VLM systems through uncertainty-weighted linear opinion pooling. Unlike prior UQ methods designed for single models, SCoOP explicitly measures collective, system-level uncertainty across multiple VLMs, enabling effective hallucination detection and abstention for highly uncertain samples. On ScienceQA, SCoOP achieves an AUROC of 0.866 for hallucination detection, outperforming baselines (0.732-0.757) by approximately 10-13%. For abstention, it attains an AURAC of 0.907, exceeding baselines (0.818-0.840) by 7-9%. Despite these gains, SCoOP introduces only microsecond-level aggregation overhead relative to the baselines, which is trivial compared to typical VLM inference time (on the order of seconds). These results demonstrate that SCoOP provides an efficient and principled mechanism for uncertainty-aware aggregation, advancing the reliability of multimodal AI systems.

TL;DR: 论文分析了生成式AI在法律领域应用中的危险失效模式：AI会伪造看似真实的判例、法规和司法观点，律师若不知情地提交这些伪造内容将面临职业风险，而法院则面临对抗程序完整性的新威胁。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文采用基于物理学的Transformer核心机制分析，揭示了AI内部状态存在可计算的阈值，当超过该阈值时，AI输出会从可靠的法律推理转变为权威性的伪造内容。研究通过模拟法律简报起草场景来展示这一科学原理，并提出用基于系统实际失效方式的验证协议替代过时的"黑箱"思维模型。

Result: 分析表明，伪造风险不是异常故障，而是技术设计的可预见后果，对技术能力义务的演变具有直接影响。AI的伪造行为具有确定性成分，其内部状态存在可计算的阈值，超过该阈值就会导致输出从可靠推理转变为权威性伪造。

Conclusion: 法律专业人士、法院和监管机构需要用基于系统实际失效方式的验证协议替代过时的"黑箱"思维模型。伪造风险是技术设计的可预见后果，而非随机异常，这对法律职业的技术能力义务提出了新的要求。

Abstract: The adoption of generative AI across commercial and legal professions offers dramatic efficiency gains -- yet for law in particular, it introduces a perilous failure mode in which the AI fabricates fictitious case law, statutes, and judicial holdings that appear entirely authentic. Attorneys who unknowingly file such fabrications face professional sanctions, malpractice exposure, and reputational harm, while courts confront a novel threat to the integrity of the adversarial process. This failure mode is commonly dismissed as random `hallucination', but recent physics-based analysis of the Transformer's core mechanism reveals a deterministic component: the AI's internal state can cross a calculable threshold, causing its output to flip from reliable legal reasoning to authoritative-sounding fabrication. Here we present this science in a legal-industry setting, walking through a simulated brief-drafting scenario. Our analysis suggests that fabrication risk is not an anomalous glitch but a foreseeable consequence of the technology's design, with direct implications for the evolving duty of technological competence. We propose that legal professionals, courts, and regulators replace the outdated `black box' mental model with verification protocols based on how these systems actually fail.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: DeepXube is a free and open-source Python package and command-line tool that seeks to automate the solution of pathfinding problems by using machine learning to learn heuristic functions that guide heuristic search algorithms tailored to deep neural networks (DNNs). DeepXube is comprised of the latest advances in deep reinforcement learning, heuristic search, and formal logic for solving pathfinding problems. This includes limited-horizon Bellman-based learning, hindsight experience replay, batched heuristic search, and specifying goals with answer-set programming. A robust multiple-inheritance structure simplifies the definition of pathfinding domains and the generation of training data. Training heuristic functions is made efficient through the automatic parallelization of the generation of training data across central processing units (CPUs) and reinforcement learning updates across graphics processing units (GPUs). Pathfinding algorithms that take advantage of the parallelism of GPUs and DNN architectures, such as batch weighted A* and Q* search and beam search are easily employed to solve pathfinding problems through command-line arguments. Finally, several convenient features for visualization, code profiling, and progress monitoring during training and solving are available. The GitHub repository is publicly available at https://github.com/forestagostinelli/deepxube.

### [34] [DUPLEX: Agentic Dual-System Planning via LLM-Driven Information Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23909)
*Keru Hua,Ding Wang,Yaoying Gu,Xiaoguang Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DUPLEX：一种双系统神经符号架构，严格限制LLM仅用于模式引导的信息提取，而非端到端规划，将逻辑规划留给符号规划器


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在机器人任务规划中具有语义灵活性，但存在幻觉和逻辑不一致问题，限制了其在长期视野领域的可靠性。需要弥合非结构化环境与严格规划综合之间的差距。

Method: 提出DUPLEX双系统神经符号架构：1）快速系统使用轻量级LLM从自然语言中提取实体、关系等，确定性地映射到PDDL问题文件供经典符号规划器使用；2）仅当规划失败时激活慢速系统，利用求解器诊断驱动高容量LLM进行迭代反思和修复。

Result: 在12个经典和家庭规划领域的广泛评估表明，DUPLEX在成功率和可靠性方面显著优于现有的端到端和混合LLM基线方法。

Conclusion: 关键不是让LLM规划得更好，而是将其限制在擅长的部分——结构化语义基础——将逻辑规划综合留给符号规划器。这种严格分工的方法显著提高了可靠性和成功率。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) provide semantic flexibility for robotic task planning, their susceptibility to hallucination and logical inconsistency limits their reliability in long-horizon domains. To bridge the gap between unstructured environments and rigorous plan synthesis, we propose DUPLEX, an agentic dual-system neuro-symbolic architecture that strictly confines the LLM to schema-guided information extraction rather than end-to-end planning or code generation. In our framework, a feed-forward Fast System utilizes a lightweight LLM to extract entities, relations etc. from natural language, deterministically mapping them into a Planning Domain Definition Language (PDDL) problem file for a classical symbolic planner. To resolve complex or underspecified scenarios, a Slow System is activated exclusively upon planning failure, leveraging solver diagnostics to drive a high-capacity LLM in iterative reflection and repair. Extensive evaluations across 12 classical and household planning domains demonstrate that DUPLEX significantly outperforms existing end-to-end and hybrid LLM baselines in both success rate and reliability. These results confirm that The key is not to make the LLM plan better, but to restrict the LLM to the part it is good at - structured semantic grounding - and leave logical plan synthesis to a symbolic planner.

AnalogAgent coordinates a Code Generator, Design Optimizer, and Knowledge Curator to distill execution feedback into an adaptive playbook in SEM and retrieve targeted guidance for subsequent generation, enabling cross-task transfer without additional expert feedback, databases, or libraries. Across established benchmarks, AnalogAgent achieves 92% Pass@1 with Gemini and 97.4% Pass@1 with GPT-5. Moreover, with compact models (e.g., Qwen-8B), it yields a +48.8% average Pass@1 gain across tasks and reaches 72.1% Pass@1 overall, indicating that AnalogAgent substantially strengthens open-weight models for high-quality analog circuit design automation.

TL;DR: 该研究通过大规模数据驱动方法分析强化学习环境的演变，揭示了从孤立物理模拟到语言驱动基础智能体的范式转变，并识别出"语义先验"和"领域特定泛化"两大生态系统。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习的进展与环境密切相关，但现有研究多为定性分析。本研究旨在通过大规模数据驱动的实证调查，量化分析RL环境的演变轨迹，为下一代环境设计提供科学依据。

Method: 1) 程序化处理大规模学术文献语料库，从2000多篇核心文献中提取数据；2) 提出多维度分类法，系统分析基准测试的应用领域和认知能力需求；3) 实施自动化的语义和统计分析，识别范式转变。

Result: 1) 发现RL环境从孤立物理模拟向通用语言驱动基础智能体的显著转变；2) 识别出两大生态系统分化："语义先验"生态系统（以大语言模型为主导）和"领域特定泛化"生态系统；3) 揭示了跨任务协同、多领域干扰和零样本泛化的"认知指纹"机制。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了量化路线图，用于设计下一代具身语义模拟器，弥合连续物理控制与高层逻辑推理之间的鸿沟，为RL环境发展提供数据验证的科学指导。

Abstract: The remarkable progress of reinforcement learning (RL) is intrinsically tied to the environments used to train and evaluate artificial agents. Moving beyond traditional qualitative reviews, this work presents a large-scale, data-driven empirical investigation into the evolution of RL environments. By programmatically processing a massive corpus of academic literature and rigorously distilling over 2,000 core publications, we propose a quantitative methodology to map the transition from isolated physical simulations to generalist, language-driven foundation agents. Implementing a novel, multi-dimensional taxonomy, we systematically analyze benchmarks against diverse application domains and requisite cognitive capabilities. Our automated semantic and statistical analysis reveals a profound, data-verified paradigm shift: the bifurcation of the field into a "Semantic Prior" ecosystem dominated by Large Language Models (LLMs) and a "Domain-Specific Generalization" ecosystem. Furthermore, we characterize the "cognitive fingerprints" of these distinct domains to uncover the underlying mechanisms of cross-task synergy, multi-domain interference, and zero-shot generalization. Ultimately, this study offers a rigorous, quantitative roadmap for designing the next generation of Embodied Semantic Simulators, bridging the gap between continuous physical control and high-level logical reasoning.

### [38] [ELITE: Experiential Learning and Intent-Aware Transfer for Self-improving Embodied Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24018)
*Bingqing Wei,Zhongyu Xia,Dingai Liu,Xiaoyu Zhou,Zhiwei Lin,Yongtao Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ELITE框架通过经验学习和意图感知迁移，使基于视觉语言模型的具身智能体能够从环境交互中持续学习，并将知识迁移到程序相似的任务中，显著提升任务执行性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于视觉语言模型（VLM）的具身智能体在复杂任务中表现不佳，经常跳过关键步骤、提出无效动作和重复错误。这是因为VLM的静态训练数据与具身任务所需的物理交互之间存在根本性差距。VLM能从静态数据中学习丰富的语义知识，但缺乏与世界交互的能力。

Method: ELITE框架包含两个协同机制：1）自反思知识构建：从执行轨迹中提取可重用策略，通过结构化精炼操作维护不断演化的策略池；2）意图感知检索：从策略池中识别相关策略并将其应用于当前任务。该框架使智能体能够从自身环境交互经验中持续学习，并将获得的知识迁移到程序相似的任务中。

Result: 在EB-ALFRED和EB-Habitat基准测试中，ELITE在无监督的在线设置下比基础VLM性能分别提升9%和5%。在有监督设置下，ELITE能有效泛化到未见过的任务类别，相比最先进的基于训练的方法获得更好的性能。

Conclusion: ELITE通过经验学习和意图感知迁移，有效弥合了语义理解和可靠动作执行之间的差距，为基于VLM的具身智能体提供了持续学习和知识迁移的有效框架。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) have shown remarkable general capabilities, yet embodied agents built on them fail at complex tasks, often skipping critical steps, proposing invalid actions, and repeating mistakes. These failures arise from a fundamental gap between the static training data of VLMs and the physical interaction for embodied tasks. VLMs can learn rich semantic knowledge from static data but lack the ability to interact with the world. To address this issue, we introduce ELITE, an embodied agent framework with {E}xperiential {L}earning and {I}ntent-aware {T}ransfer that enables agents to continuously learn from their own environment interaction experiences, and transfer acquired knowledge to procedurally similar tasks. ELITE operates through two synergistic mechanisms, \textit{i.e.,} self-reflective knowledge construction and intent-aware retrieval. Specifically, self-reflective knowledge construction extracts reusable strategies from execution trajectories and maintains an evolving strategy pool through structured refinement operations. Then, intent-aware retrieval identifies relevant strategies from the pool and applies them to current tasks. Experiments on the EB-ALFRED and EB-Habitat benchmarks show that ELITE achieves 9\% and 5\% performance improvement over base VLMs in the online setting without any supervision. In the supervised setting, ELITE generalizes effectively to unseen task categories, achieving better performance compared to state-of-the-art training-based methods. These results demonstrate the effectiveness of ELITE for bridging the gap between semantic understanding and reliable action execution.

### [39] [Enhanced Mycelium of Thought (EMoT): A Bio-Inspired Hierarchical Reasoning Architecture with Strategic Dormancy and Mnemonic Encoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24065)
*Florian Odi Stummer*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: EMoT是一种受生物启发的推理框架，采用四层层次结构（微观、中观、宏观、元认知），结合战略休眠、记忆宫殿和五种记忆编码风格，专门针对复杂多领域问题设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM提示范式（如CoT和ToT）采用线性或树状推理路径，缺乏持久记忆、战略休眠和跨领域综合能力，无法有效处理复杂多领域问题。

Method: 提出EMoT框架：1）四层认知层次结构（Micro, Meso, Macro, Meta）；2）推理节点的战略休眠与重新激活机制；3）记忆宫殿与五种记忆编码风格（视觉、听觉、语义、情感、空间）集成。

Result: 在盲评LLM-as-Judge评估中，EMoT与CoT表现接近（4.20 vs 4.33/5.0）但稳定性更高，在跨领域综合任务上优于CoT（4.8 vs 4.4）。战略休眠是关键架构要素（禁用后质量从4.2降至1.0）。但在15项简答题基准测试中表现不佳（27%），确认对简单问题存在系统性过度思考。

Conclusion: EMoT是首个结合层次拓扑、战略休眠与重新激活、记忆编码的推理框架，专门针对复杂多领域问题而非通用提示增强。存在样本量小、LLM-as-Judge评估偏差、33倍计算成本等限制，在简单问题上表现不佳但复杂问题上有潜力。

Abstract: Current prompting paradigms for large language models (LLMs), including Chain-of-Thought (CoT) and Tree-of-Thoughts (ToT), follow linear or tree-structured reasoning paths that lack persistent memory, strategic dormancy, and cross-domain synthesis. We present the Enhanced Mycelium of Thought (EMoT) framework, a bio-inspired reasoning architecture that organises cognitive processing into a four-level hierarchy (Micro, Meso, Macro, Meta), implements strategic dormancy and reactivation of reasoning nodes, and integrates a Memory Palace with five mnemonic encoding styles. EMoT is a research prototype for complex, multi-domain problems, not a general-purpose prompting enhancement. Two complementary evaluations reveal a characteristic trade-off. In a blind LLM-as-Judge evaluation across three domains, EMoT achieved near-parity with CoT (4.20 vs. 4.33/5.0) with higher stability, and outperformed CoT on Cross-Domain Synthesis (4.8 vs. 4.4). Ablation studies show that strategic dormancy is architecturally essential (quality collapsed from 4.2 to 1.0 when disabled). On a 15-item short-answer benchmark, EMoT (27%) substantially underperformed simpler baselines, confirming systematic overthinking on simple problems. These results are subject to important limitations: small sample sizes (n=3 complex cases, n=15 short-answer items), LLM-as-Judge evaluation with potential self-preference bias, and approximately 33-fold computational cost overhead. To our knowledge, EMoT is the first reasoning framework to combine hierarchical topology, strategic thought dormancy with reactivation, and mnemonic memory encoding in a single architecture.

To address this, we introduce the first comprehensive, standardized benchmark suite for exact and approximate MOS. Our suite spans four structurally diverse domains: real-world road networks, structured synthetic graphs, game-based grid environments, and high-dimensional robotic motion-planning roadmaps. By providing fixed graph instances, standardized start-goal queries, and both exact and approximate reference Pareto-optimal solution sets, this suite captures a full spectrum of objective interactions: from strongly correlated to strictly independent. Ultimately, this benchmark provides a common foundation to ensure future MOS evaluations are robust, reproducible, and structurally comprehensive.

*Yunbo Long*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AutoProf是一个多智能体编排框架，通过维护持续演化的研究世界模型（知识图谱）实现端到端的AI研究监督，支持从文献综述到论文撰写的完整研究流程，具有结构化差距发现、自校正发现循环和自我改进开发循环三大核心贡献。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: AutoProf采用多智能体编排框架，维护持续演化的研究世界模型（知识图谱）作为共享记忆。包含三大核心方法：1) 结构化差距发现：将方法分解为模块，跨基准评估并识别模块级差距；2) 自校正发现循环：分析模块成功/失败原因，检测基准偏差，评估评估充分性；3) 自我改进开发循环：使用跨领域机制搜索迭代解决失败组件。所有智能体在共识机制下运行，验证发现后才提交到共享模型。

Result: AutoProf是一个模型无关的框架，支持主流大语言模型，能够根据token预算弹性扩展，从轻量级探索到全面调查。框架实现了端到端的AI研究监督，从文献综述到论文撰写，通过自主探索和自我校正更新驱动研究过程。

Conclusion: AutoProf通过多智能体编排和持续演化的研究世界模型，解决了现有自动化研究系统的局限性，实现了结构化差距发现、自校正和自我改进的研究流程，为端到端AI研究监督提供了可扩展的框架。

Abstract: Existing automated research systems operate as stateless, linear pipelines, generating outputs without maintaining a persistent understanding of the research landscape. They process papers sequentially, propose ideas without structured gap analysis, and lack mechanisms for agents to verify or refine each other's findings. We present AutoProf (Autonomous Professor), a multi-agent orchestration framework where specialized agents provide end-to-end AI research supervision driven by human interests, from literature review through gap discovery, method development, evaluation, and paper writing, via autonomous exploration and self-correcting updates. Unlike sequential pipelines, AutoProf maintains a continuously evolving Research World Model implemented as a Knowledge Graph, capturing methods, benchmarks, limitations, and unexplored gaps as shared memory across agents. The framework introduces three contributions: first, structured gap discovery that decomposes methods into modules, evaluates them across benchmarks, and identifies module-level gaps; second, self-correcting discovery loops that analyze why modules succeed or fail, detect benchmark biases, and assess evaluation adequacy; third, self-improving development loops using cross-domain mechanism search to iteratively address failing components. All agents operate under a consensus mechanism where findings are validated before being committed to the shared model. The framework is model-agnostic, supports mainstream large language models, and scales elastically with token budget from lightweight exploration to full-scale investigation.

### [42] [Multi-Agent Reasoning with Consistency Verification Improves Uncertainty Calibration in Medical MCQA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24481)
*John Ray B. Martinez*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 多智能体框架通过领域专家智能体、两阶段验证和S分数加权融合，显著改善医学多选题回答的校准性和判别能力，ECE降低49-74%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在临床环境中部署AI时，校准不良的置信度分数是一个实际障碍。总是过度自信的模型无法为临床延迟决策提供有用信号，需要改进校准性和判别能力。

Method: 提出多智能体框架：1) 四个领域专家智能体（呼吸、心脏、神经、胃肠）使用Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct生成独立诊断；2) 两阶段自验证过程测量内部一致性并产生专家置信分数(S-score)；3) S分数驱动的加权融合策略选择最终答案并校准报告的置信度。

Result: 在MedQA-USMLE和MedMCQA的四个实验设置中，ECE降低49-74%。在MedQA-250上，完整系统达到ECE=0.091（比单专家基线降低74.4%），AUROC=0.630（+0.056），准确率59.2%。消融分析显示两阶段验证是主要校准驱动因素，多智能体推理是主要准确率驱动因素。

Conclusion: 基于一致性的验证能够为不同医学问题类型产生更可靠的不确定性估计，为安全关键的临床AI应用中的延迟决策提供实用的置信度信号。

Abstract: Miscalibrated confidence scores are a practical obstacle to deploying AI in clinical settings. A model that is always overconfident offers no useful signal for deferral. We present a multi-agent framework that combines domain-specific specialist agents with Two-Phase Verification and S-Score Weighted Fusion to improve both calibration and discrimination in medical multiple-choice question answering. Four specialist agents (respiratory, cardiology, neurology, gastroenterology) generate independent diagnoses using Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct. Each diagnosis is then subjected to a two-phase self-verification process that measures internal consistency and produces a Specialist Confidence Score (S-score). The S-scores drive a weighted fusion strategy that selects the final answer and calibrates the reported confidence. We evaluate across four experimental settings, covering 100-question and 250-question high-disagreement subsets of both MedQA-USMLE and MedMCQA. Calibration improvement is the central finding, with ECE reduced by 49-74% across all four settings, including the harder MedMCQA benchmark where these gains persist even when absolute accuracy is constrained by knowledge-intensive recall demands. On MedQA-250, the full system achieves ECE = 0.091 (74.4% reduction over the single-specialist baseline) and AUROC = 0.630 (+0.056) at 59.2% accuracy. Ablation analysis identifies Two-Phase Verification as the primary calibration driver and multi-agent reasoning as the primary accuracy driver. These results establish that consistency-based verification produces more reliable uncertainty estimates across diverse medical question types, providing a practical confidence signal for deferral in safety-critical clinical AI applications.
